Alpha males are massive predators with thicker hide and more powerful attacks, while matriarch females are the mothers of the pack and lay eggs to continue the species. Both are incredibly deadly and nearly impossible to tame.</FCP_Animal_Alpha_Deathclaw.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Beachlurk.description>A coastal variant of the mirelurk that has adapted to sandy beach environments. These creatures have lighter-colored shells that blend with beach sand, making them harder to spot until they emerge from the surf. Beachlurks are slightly more aggressive than their swamp-dwelling cousins and often bury themselves in sand to ambush prey.</FCP_Animal_Beachlurk.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Bighorner.description>A mutated descendant of bighorn sheep. These hardy creatures are commonly used as pack animals and livestock throughout the wasteland, valued for their strength, meat, and hide. Males sport impressive curved horns and are larger and more aggressive than females.</FCP_Animal_Bighorner.description>
  <FCP_Animal_Bighorner.label>bighorner</FCP_Animal_Bighorner.label>
  <FCP_Animal_Deathclaw.description>A large, agile, and powerful creature with deadly claws, the deathclaw is the most fearsome predator of the wasteland. Created through pre-war genetic engineering, these apex predators are incredibly dangerous and nearly impossible to tame. They hunt in packs and can tear through armor with ease.</FCP_Animal_Deathclaw.description>
  <FCP_Animal_Deathclaw.label>Deathclaw</FCP_Animal_Deathclaw.label>
  <FCP_Animal_Fire_Gecko.description>A dangerous mutated gecko with the ability to breathe fire. These fearsome creatures have developed specialized glands that allow them to expel flames at their enemies. Fire geckos are highly aggressive and territorial, making them extremely dangerous to encounter in the wild. Their unique physiology makes them resistant to heat and fire, and their hide is particularly valuable. They are typically found in hot, desert regions.</FCP_Animal_Fire_Gecko.description>
  <FCP_Animal_Fire_Gecko.label>Fire Gecko</FCP_Animal_Fire_Gecko.label>

  <FCP_Animal_Gecko.description>A large mutated gecko that has grown to the size of a small dog. These reptilian creatures are common throughout the wasteland, particularly in desert regions. While not particularly aggressive, they will defend themselves when threatened. Their meat is edible and their hide makes decent leather.</FCP_Animal_Gecko.description>
  <FCP_Animal_Gecko.label>Gecko</FCP_Animal_Gecko.label>
  <FCP_Animal_German_Shepherd_Dog.description>Some dogs are wild, plaguing the wastes and killing livestock, but tame versions are necessary for many struggling wastelanders. There are also rare cases of domestic breeds that act as companions towards their bipedal counterparts. Humans and super mutants are the only species known to truly tame and domesticate these canines.</FCP_Animal_German_Shepherd_Dog.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Giant_Mantis.description>A heavily mutated praying mantis grown to enormous size by prolonged radiation exposure. These aggressive predators hunt with lightning-fast reflexes and devastating raptorial forelegs capable of impaling prey in a single strike. Their chitinous exoskeleton provides considerable protection, and they're known to be territorial and highly aggressive when threatened. Found primarily in arid regions where they ambush unsuspecting victims.</FCP_Animal_Giant_Mantis.description>

Prolonged exposure to radiation has made these creatures larger and more aggressive than normal radstags. Their meat is highly radioactive and dangerous to consume, but their glowing presence makes them easy to spot at night.</FCP_Animal_Glowing_Radstag.description>

These creatures are prized for their valuable hide, which can be crafted into high-quality leather goods. Golden geckos are stronger and more aggressive than their common cousins, and their bite can deliver a mild poison. They are found in desert regions and rocky terrain.</FCP_Animal_Golden_Gecko.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Green_Gecko.description>A large mutated gecko with green scales and a more aggressive temperament than common geckos. Green geckos are tougher and more dangerous, with a stronger bite that can deliver toxins. They are commonly found in rocky areas and caves throughout the wasteland. Their hide is valuable and their meat is edible, though it must be properly prepared.</FCP_Animal_Green_Gecko.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Lakelurk.description>A highly evolved mutant creature that combines features of snapping turtles and cuttlefish. Unlike mirelurks, lakelurks are much more aggressive and possess a sonic attack that can disorient prey. Their shells are extremely tough, and they're far more intelligent than other lurk variants. Found primarily in large lakes and deep waters, they're apex aquatic predators of the wasteland.</FCP_Animal_Lakelurk.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Lakelurk_King.description>A massive male lakelurk that has grown to enormous proportions. Lakelurk kings are territorial apex predators that claim entire lakes as their domain. They possess enhanced sonic abilities that can stun multiple targets, incredibly thick shells, and devastating strength. These solitary giants are always male and highly aggressive, attacking anything that enters their territory. Extremely rare and highly dangerous.</FCP_Animal_Lakelurk_King.description>

There are also rare cases of domestic breeds such as German Shepherds act as companions towards their bipedal counterparts. The Minutemen around the ruins of Boston in particular have used them as working and guard dogs for their military.</FCP_Animal_Minutemen_Guard_Dog.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Mirelurk.description>A heavily mutated crustacean that has grown to enormous size. These creatures have thick, chitinous shells that provide excellent protection against most weapons. Mirelurks are territorial and aggressive, using their powerful claws to defend their nesting grounds. They're typically found near bodies of water and coastal areas, scavenging for food and defending their territory with surprising ferocity.</FCP_Animal_Mirelurk.description>
  <FCP_Animal_Mirelurk.label>Mirelurk</FCP_Animal_Mirelurk.label>

  <FCP_Animal_Mirelurk_King.description>Despite its name, the mirelurk king is not actually a mirelurk at all. This towering bipedal predator is believed to be a heavily mutated Jackson's chameleon, sharing no direct relation to the crustacean-like mirelurks. The name comes from their tendency to inhabit areas near mirelurk colonies. Kings stand on two legs, possess powerful clawed hands, and can emit devastating sonic screams. Their exposed flesh and lack of a protective shell is compensated by remarkable agility and deadly close-range attacks.</FCP_Animal_Mirelurk_King.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Molerat.description>A grotesque mutated rodent that has grown to an unusually large size. These hairless, aggressive creatures are common throughout the wasteland, particularly in underground areas and ruins. They travel in packs and will attack anything that enters their territory. Their meat is barely edible and their hide is nearly worthless, but they breed rapidly and can overwhelm unprepared travelers.</FCP_Animal_Molerat.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Nightstalker.description>A horrifying product of pre-war genetic experimentation, the nightstalker is a hybrid creature combining the DNA of coyotes and rattlesnakes. These stealthy predators hunt in packs under cover of darkness, using their venomous bite to bring down prey. They possess the pack intelligence of canines combined with the stealth and venom of serpents, making them one of the wasteland's most feared predators. Their distinctive silhouette and glowing eyes strike terror into those who encounter them.</FCP_Animal_Nightstalker.description>

These large black birds are known for their intelligence and adaptability, often following travelers and raiders to feed on carrion. While they prefer scavenging, rad ravens are capable predators that hunt small creatures. They can be trained to a useful degree, making them valuable companions for wasteland scouts.</FCP_Animal_Rad_Raven.description>

  <FCP_Animal_Radgull.description>A hardy seabird that has adapted remarkably well to the irradiated coasts of the wasteland. These gregarious birds travel in large flocks, their distinctive calls echoing across contaminated shorelines. Radgulls are highly resistant to radiation and can eat almost anything, making them successful scavengers. They're commonly found along coastal areas where they dive for mutated fish and pick through debris. With intermediate intelligence, they can be trained for various tasks.</FCP_Animal_Radgull.description>
